  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_bcabf501-a803-44f1-aa83-8ad5c6a33abe'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

<span id="freeTextContainer2810259275915351155">It's been twelve years since Tru Bennett last saw Jake Wethers, her former best friend and boy she once loved.<br/><br/>Jake Wethers, sexy, tattooed and deliciously bad lead singer, and brains behind The Mighty Storm, one of the biggest bands in the world, left Tru with a broken heart when he moved from England to America with his family when they were both fourteen.<br/><br/>Sent to intervie</span>
  <span id="freeText2810259275915351155" style="display:none">It's been twelve years since Tru Bennett last saw Jake Wethers, her former best friend and boy she once loved.<br /><br />Jake Wethers, sexy, tattooed and deliciously bad lead singer, and brains behind The Mighty Storm, one of the biggest bands in the world, left Tru with a broken heart when he moved from England to America with his family when they were both fourteen.<br /><br />Sent to interview Jake for her music column by the magazine she works for, they are both unprepared for the sparks that fly the instant they reconnect. Only, there’s a complication to their instant feelings for one another—Will, Tru’s boyfriend of two years. <br /><br />Then Jake makes Tru a job offer she can't refuse—travelling the world with him and his band. But taking the job means leaving Will behind, and being on the road with the band means spending an inordinate amount of time with Jake. <br /><br />Is Tru strong enough to resist the delectable bad boy who once held her heart so completely, or will she willingly risk it all for one night with the world's most notorious womanizer?</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer401107830" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1261513464415588603"><b>2 stars</b><br/><br/>Looks like this is another one of those books everyone loves but me. I desperately tried and wanted to love this story like many of its readers, but, ultimately, this book did not work for me. <br/><br/>My biggest issue with this story, besides the long-winded, and, frankly, amateurish and disjointed prose, was the author's tendency to tell me what to feel rather than allowing me to experience it myself. When the prose managed to flow smoothly and passionately, it felt effortless and I easily becam</span>
  <span id="freeText1261513464415588603" style="display:none"><b>2 stars</b><br /><br />Looks like this is another one of those books everyone loves but me. I desperately tried and wanted to love this story like many of its readers, but, ultimately, this book did not work for me. <br /><br />My biggest issue with this story, besides the long-winded, and, frankly, amateurish and disjointed prose, was the author's tendency to tell me what to feel rather than allowing me to experience it myself. When the prose managed to flow smoothly and passionately, it felt effortless and I easily became immersed in Tru and Jake's world; unfortunately, that happened rarely. I was relieved as the story progressed that the excessive rhetoric did slowly taper off–the author stopped give us the complete rundown of the characters every move and action–but not enough to redeem the story for me. <br /><br />I also had a difficult time with the cheating aspect in this book, but not for the reasons I expected. I expected to feel upset and somewhat disgusted with the characters. What I ended up feeling, however, was indifference. I was completely detached from the drama of the situation. I had to constantly remind myself that Tru was seriously involved with someone else. I felt her relationship with her boyfriend, Will, was manufactured and insubstantial. Making what should have caused me emotional turmoil inconsequential. I did roll my eyes at Tru's hypocrisy when she believed Jake, the hero, cheated on her. Now that did annoy me! <br /><br />I know many readers love this book and I understand why–it's full of intrigue, drama, and spice. For me, however, this became a story that had great potential but got lost in it's own rhetoric. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1261513464415588603" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_400197084" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/400197084" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/400197084?book_show_action=true">Aug 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer400197084" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13931813436798345103"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388985i/749912._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i> <b> “I love you… I’ve only ever loved one girl, Tru – and that’s you. It’s always been you. I’ve loved you from the moment I knew how to love.“ </b></i><br/><br/><b> *SQUEEEEE* ABSOLUTELY AMAZING ROCKSTAR ROMANCE!!! WOW! </b><br/><br/>I am totally in LOVE with this book! Freaking. Thrilling. Read.<br/><br/>A well-written, beautiful story that put me through a deliciously emotional angsty ringer, made my heart race and flutter and had me swooning like crazy over Jake Wethers.<br/><br/>I loved the writing style right from the start. It was vivid, clean,</span>
  <span id="freeText13931813436798345103" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388985i/749912._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> <b> “I love you… I’ve only ever loved one girl, Tru – and that’s you. It’s always been you. I’ve loved you from the moment I knew how to love.“ </b></i><br><br><b> *SQUEEEEE* ABSOLUTELY AMAZING ROCKSTAR ROMANCE!!! WOW! </b><br><br>I am totally in LOVE with this book! Freaking. Thrilling. Read.<br><br>A well-written, beautiful story that put me through a deliciously emotional angsty ringer, made my heart race and flutter and had me swooning like crazy over Jake Wethers.<br><br>I loved the writing style right from the start. It was vivid, clean, and got you right into Tru’s head. This book made me laugh, cry, squee, cheer, gasp, sigh, swoon, melt, fan myself, take deep calming breaths in order to move on, gave me goosbumps, made my breath hitch, made me read with misty eyes for like the whole final 15%, it just TOTALLY affected me. My emotions were all over the place and all of them were INTENSE!<br><br>My heart = the author’s yo-yo. I utterly LOVED IT!!<br><br>Tru and Jake were the best of childhood friends. They did everything together. And although they were too young to really understand it, they did fall in love. Everything was perfect until his family suddenly uprouted to a different country when they were 14 and they lost touch.<br><br>Now, twelve years later, Jake has become the world famous ”ultimate bad boy of rock” – living a life full of booze, parties, drugs and women , while Tru has become a music journalist. Even though he’s hugely popular, she’s never told anyone that she knew him, wanting to keep that part of her memories private. So now, when her boss signs her up to interview and write an article on him, she absolutely terrified – she knows he’s changed from the boy she knew – will he remember her? What will they say? She knows about a dark part of his past that the world does’t now about. Maybe he won’t want to see her? And yet at the same time, she’s utterly excited out of her mind.<br><br> <i> <b>“Jake Wethers, the man who used to be the boy I loved.” </b></i> <br><br>Ooooooohhmigosh, when they meet for the first time again, my. heart. was. racing!!!! I was smiling, grinning, and my heart was pounding. It was AMAZING!! I love books that affect me so strongly and I have to say that from the moment I met Jake, I fell in instant love with him. INSTANT.<br><br>And its clear from the start that the spark between them has never died. And he asks her to go on tour with them as the official biographer of his tour and then oh how the fun begins as Jake, subtly at first, and later not so subtly, works hard to rekindle the romance and show Tru the depths of the feelings he’s always had for her.<br><br><i> <b> “It’s always been you, Tru. Always.” </b></i>  *melt*”<br><br>Now, here’s the hiccup, Tru has a boyfriend, Will- a wonderful, sweet, gorgeous, loving boyfriend. And dispite her feelings towards Jake, she isn’t quite sure how he feels towards her. She has a lot of insecurities, but I found them to be understandable – annoying perhaps at times because of how badly I just wanted them to get together, but they were not ridiculous. I think its easy for people on the outside to judge her initial reaction, but honestly, in her shoes, I’d prolly be having a lot of the same thoughts myself.<br><br>There IS a little bit of a love triangle going on for a part of the book, and yes, when Jake and Tru first get physical, there IS cheating. But, and here’s the big BUT, it did not bother me (*gasp* and I’m the person who utterly HATES any cheating in books). Why did it not bother me? Because it wasn’t long and drawn out. The cheating was understandable. Here are two people CLEARLY meant to be together who have honestly LOVED each other since they were kids, in a sitation where one of them is attached. It sucks. And they gave what they had between them a go and ended up telling Will within a few days of starting so there wasn’t this huge big long cheating time. Yes, it was messy. My heart was in utter turmoil. Yes, my heart hurt for Will. But there was just no denying how right Jake and True felt together. They were truely each other’s soul mates.<br><br><i> <b> “You’re mine, Tru. I’m not sharing you with him anymore.” </b></i>  <br><br>And this isn’t a book about cheating. Its a story about a childhood love that never truely went away throughout years of separation, and how, once reunited, nothing will be able to keep them apart. The cheating thing gets resolved quickly and then after that its just about Jake and Tru.<br><br>So, now, back to Jake *pauses a moment to SWOON*… Jake Wethers, perhaps the sweetest and hottest rock god to grace this earth. I have’t had my heart this much a-flutter since Kellan and Gideon. Let me tell you, I was hyperventilating and swooning to the MAX. What is it about rock stars that is just so. Freaking. THRILLING?!<br><br>The chemistry between Jake and Tru… oh dear lord *fans self*, it sizzles. You can feel it come right off the page. Totally undiable. Totally INTENSE. From the start, you can just FEEL that its ’right’ between them. And the intensity between them just slowly builds from their first meeting to the point where it just couldn’t be held back any more. Made you feel for them that much more strongly.<br><br>The book is steamy – very steamy, but not erotica steamy. Its there, but not overpowering. Personally, I thought it was just the right amount for this story.<br><br>Once Jake and Tru were together, yes, they fought, yes, they had their moments of stupid, but c’mon, who doesn’t? Personally, despite reading some of the scenes and just going “FUUUUUUUUCCCKKKKKK”, I didn’t find that the drama overshadowed the story, but rather brought it a sense of realism. They have a lot to deal with – paparazi, public image, various things that happen in their private life… and so naturally, it affects them. But they do work through their issues… and them together just utterly melted my heart *dreamy sigh*<br><br>The pacing of the book was mostly excellent. But if I had to complain, I’d say that there were a few scenes that were alluded to, but skipped over in detail that I’d really have wished to read in full. The time jumps are a little jolting, making you momentarily disconnect from the story line, but it quickly picks up again and didn’t take away from my overall reading experience.<br><br>This book deals with a lot of serious issues – drugs, cheating, death, commitment, the effects of fame. But its a romance at heart… and an abolutely beautiful one at that.<br><br>The ending was a totally swoony HEA but was a little abrupt. I loved it, but… I WANT MORE!!!! NOW!! Please?! Ms. Towle, pretty please????!! *begs*<br><br>oooo and we are treated at the end of the book to one chapter from Jake’s POV. Its the scene where they meet for the first time and can I just say that that might actually be the BEST guy POV I’ve ever read. You got RIGHT into his head. Literally every thought. It was BRILLIANT. <br><br>The sequel will be out on August 20th, 2013 :)<br><br>If you are looking for a rockstar romance that will totally take over your heart, try this one out!<br><br>Also, if you liked this book, you will most likely love Thoughtless, and vice versa… if you are a big fan of Thoughtless, RUN out and get yourself this book. Cuz… just WOW!! <br><br>Jake Wethers… you are my rock god &lt;3<br><br>I found a picture of this guy that looks EXACTLY like how Jake was described in the books (just add blue contacts and tattoo him up a bit in your minds :P ). What do you guys think? Is he HOT or what?<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395483i/761762._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388985i/749913._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388985i/749914._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and how's this for a potential Jake and Tru?<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388985i/749915._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="13931813436798345103" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_418882034" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/418882034" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/418882034?book_show_action=true">Sep 20, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Stacia (the 2010 club) by: </span>
      My Smut Monday girls
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=will-not-continue-series">will-not-continue-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer418882034" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10684832507661022847">2.5 stars.<br/><br/><b>You are only allowed to read this review if one of these three things applies to you :</b><br/><br/>1. You've read this book.<br/>2. You have no plans of reading this book, so spoilers will not be an issue for you.<br/>3. You plan on reading the book but don't mind a few spoilers because you want to read my awesome half-assed review (okay, so the narcissism was unnecessary, but you get my point).<br/><br/><b>I'm not going to lie, I was a hair nervous to read this book.</b><br/><br/>I know that a couple of my friends on GR were involved</span>
  <span id="freeText10684832507661022847" style="display:none">2.5 stars.<br /><br /><b>You are only allowed to read this review if one of these three things applies to you :</b><br /><br />1. You've read this book.<br />2. You have no plans of reading this book, so spoilers will not be an issue for you.<br />3. You plan on reading the book but don't mind a few spoilers because you want to read my awesome half-assed review (okay, so the narcissism was unnecessary, but you get my point).<br /><br /><b>I'm not going to lie, I was a hair nervous to read this book.</b><br /><br />I know that a couple of my friends on GR were involved in some of the pre-release feedback for <i>The Mighty Storm</i> and I didn't want to piss off anyone if I hated the book because (surprise, surprise) I actually do like my friends. <br /><br /><b>So I had a few complaints, but overall, it wasn't a bad read.</b><br /><br />I'm just going to go conversational on this review...no bullet points, no pics...just talking it out here. <br /><br /><b>Let's address the first 2/3 of the story :</b><br /><br />The first 2/3 of the story felt like a better-written version of Thoughtless. The writing was more polished (other than a few typos) and there were far less repetitive character quirks and annoying habits. Because of this, I was probably less annoyed over the cheating than some people were. I'd seen it done in a far more excessive way in <i>Thoughtless,</i> so it didn't quite grate on me the same way here. I still wish that Tru had nipped things in the bud a few chapters sooner, however. I say this just about any time I read a story which features cheating as a main plot point - it's not the cheating that I have a problem with (we're all human and make mistakes), it's when the action continues <i>on and on</i> that I start to get antsy. Once or twice is not an issue for me. I'm fine with a little bit of drama thrown into a story...just don't drag it out past a point where we start to lose sympathy for the characters. <br /><br />I do think cheating as a main plot device is sort of tired by now. There are a thousand other ways to write conflict into a story without having to resort to this. Unless the author is going to bring it and expand upon the subject and make it something so major and creative that the idea blows everyone's minds, I'd rather see this trend be put to rest.<br /><br /><i>Overall, I liked Jake and Tru's chemistry.</i> I felt the connection and understood Tru's dilemma. In her situation, it was easy to see why she was torn. She had the love of a good man for 2 years, but the person she was closest to from her childhood came back. It was easy to see why she wrestled with her emotions. <br /><br />There were moments between the two of them that were magical :<br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Joder," I whisper.<br />He grabs my hair, kissing me hard on the mouth.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br />I really liked Jake. He was sexy, funny, cocky, interesting and thoughtful. His long-standing love and devotion toward Tru was adorable to watch. His issues and questionable acts of retaliation didn't really bother me because he had a lot on his plate and Tru didn't always make things easy for him (again, I've seen worse, so I tend to let things slide when some books take the behavior and amp it up way beyond this). The sex was nice and the love story was sweet. These are the things I actually didn't have a problem with.<br /><br />But yeah, there were a few moments that I could have lived without...<br /><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Now I see that Jake is my mighty storm. He's <s>fifty shades of fucked up</s> broken and complex, and no one knows him like I do, or ever will. He needs me.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br />*innocent whistle* You didn't see my revision there, right?<br /><br /><b>Now let's address the last 1/3 of the story :</b><br /><br />Honestly, I felt like the story should have ended when Jake and Tru got together the first time.<br /><br />Tackling a drug issue during the last 100 pages of the book was just rushed and somewhat sloppy. In order to really give the proper amount of focus to this, there should have been more time allotted for the second part of the story. I would have preferred to have seen this book end at the part where you "thought" a HEA was going to happen, and the second part of the story broken off into another book. Otherwise, I would have preferred to have seen Jake and Tru get together much earlier on and had less focus on Will. Perhaps there shouldn't have been a love triangle after all. These two could have reconnected, then a focus might have been put on the problems that a fledgling couple thrown into the midst of fame and paparazzi stalking would have gone through. Either way, it felt like we had two separate books clashing with each other in one binding. <br /><br /><b>Who should read this?</b><br /><br />Fans of high-drama books would probably enjoy this story. If you liked <i>Thoughtless</i>, then you'll probably find <i>Mighty Storm</i> to be a good fit. If you didn't like <i>Thoughtless</i>, but only because of the repetitiveness, then there's still a chance that you'll enjoy <i>Mighty Storm.</i> <br /><br />If you can't handle cheating in any form, then you'll want to skip this one. </span>
  <a data-text-id="10684832507661022847" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2030974283" />
    <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli"><img alt="Pearl Angeli" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588420465p2/31514572.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2030974283?book_show_action=true">Jun 16, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pearl Angeli" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>
      </span>

        rated it

<span id="freeTextContainer14379743960308723154"><b>5 <i>You're my June</i> Stars!</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“It's always been you. I loved you from the moment I knew how to love.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Choosing <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15724654.The_Mighty_Storm__The_Storm___1_' title='The Mighty Storm (The Storm, #1) by Samantha Towle' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Mighty Storm</a> as my next read was definitely the BEST decision that I've made because this is now officially added to my list of favorites!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1497832841ra/23060432.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>At first, I thought the book was just like any other rock star romances that portray typical plots about a famous guy falling in love with an ordinary girl. Well, there were certainly clichés thrown in places in this book but I could say they</span>
  <span id="freeText14379743960308723154" style="display:none"><b>5 <i>You're my June</i> Stars!</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“It's always been you. I loved you from the moment I knew how to love.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Choosing <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15724654.The_Mighty_Storm__The_Storm___1_" title="The Mighty Storm (The Storm, #1) by Samantha Towle" rel="nofollow noopener">The Mighty Storm</a> as my next read was definitely the BEST decision that I've made because this is now officially added to my list of favorites!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1497832841ra/23060432.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>At first, I thought the book was just like any other rock star romances that portray typical plots about a famous guy falling in love with an ordinary girl. Well, there were certainly clichés thrown in places in this book but I could say they were designed in a gripping, enticing way. One you couldn't say no to. <br><br>The story centers around the characters <b>Jake Wethers</b> and <b>Trudy "Tru" Bennett</b>. Jake, the lead singer and founder of one of the biggest rock bands known as <i>The Mighty Storm</i>, is dubbed as the ultimate bad boy and a prolific womanizing rock star. He was Tru's best friend (and first love) when they were still kids but after he moved to the US with his mom and stepdad, their communication stopped. After 12 years of separation, their paths crossed again when Tru interviewed Jake for a magazine scoop. Now a music journalist, Tru did not expect her feelings for Jake to reawaken after seeing him again.<br><br>The romance was intoxicating and the <b>angst</b> was so good I devoured it all up. There were a lot of scenes that made me feel anxious and totally on edge while waiting for what's about to happen between Tru and Jake. There were also parts that made me feel furious because of Tru's stupid decisions. I have to admit that Tru got on my nerves most of the time. Surprisingly though, her annoying qualities didn't diminish my overall enjoyment because I just loved how the story was beautifully rendered. <br><br>Call me shallow, but one of the things that I also loved about this book was Jake Wethers. Book boyfriend alert, ladies and gentlemen! <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1497832346ra/23060416.gif" width="350" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>If you fancy bad boy and possessive (in a good way) heroes, I don't think you will ever dislike Jake. I loved how his character was portrayed here. He's this kind of guy that's too good to be true despite his flaws and imperfections.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I love you beyond any lyrics I could ever write, or any words I could ever say.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>What an emotional journey <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15724654.The_Mighty_Storm__The_Storm___1_" title="The Mighty Storm (The Storm, #1) by Samantha Towle" rel="nofollow noopener">The Mighty Storm</a> has been. I just love Tru and Jake together! I wish to read more books like this, books that will make me feel like I am reading a romance book for the very first time. You know that feeling? Ughhh...<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“To me Jake was and is music, it's what glued us together.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <p>
    <a href="https://pagesofpearl.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer11574403807563681053"><b>5 SMOKING HOT JAKETASTIC STARS</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>STOP WHAT YOU'RE READING AND READ THIS NOW!!!!!!!!!</i>
</b><br/><br/>This book was so much more than a 5 Star Book! In-fact I don't think there's a rating high enough for it. <b>YES!!!</b> It was that freaking good!!!! Lets start somewhere absolutely delicious! I'm talking about Rock God extraordinaire, Jake freaking Wethers!!!! He's the quintessential bad boy, tattoo's, lean body, cocky, sexy, the whole damn package! He's the type of bad boy that immediately gives you flutters in your </span>
  <span id="freeText11574403807563681053" style="display:none"><b>5 SMOKING HOT JAKETASTIC STARS</b><br><br><b>
  <i>STOP WHAT YOU'RE READING AND READ THIS NOW!!!!!!!!!</i>
</b><br><br>This book was so much more than a 5 Star Book! In-fact I don't think there's a rating high enough for it. <b>YES!!!</b> It was that freaking good!!!! Lets start somewhere absolutely delicious! I'm talking about Rock God extraordinaire, Jake freaking Wethers!!!! He's the quintessential bad boy, tattoo's, lean body, cocky, sexy, the whole damn package! He's the type of bad boy that immediately gives you flutters in your tummy and I'm not talking little pitter patters, I'm talking <b>FULL BLOWN FLUTTERS!!!</b> Your girly parts will never be the same. <br><br><b>
  <i>"Well, when we're talking sex and you, baby, my clothes just disintegrate," he shrugs, grinning. ~~ Jake</i>
</b><br><br>Yes my friends that is a "Jake" quote! I know totally bad boy hot right?!<br><br>Jake and Trudy grew up together in the Uk and were best friends. They were separated because Jakes family landed up moving to the US when he was 14. And of course they run into each other again when Trudy Bennett (aka Tru) who is a music journalist, comes and interview's Jake for a column at the magazine she is working at. The chemistry between these two is palpable and intense!! And after they run into each other the story just takes off! This book had everything in it, one minute you are happy and dancing around and the next you are anxious and tense and then thirty seconds after that you are in tears and are crying like a baby! It was a rainbow of emotions and was so good to read. Samantha's book are always such a journey and roller coaster ride and this one was no different. Jake wins you over immediately and worms his way into your heart and you fall in love with Tru even with all the stupid decisions she makes!!<br><br>If you're looking for something sexy, angsty and just plain EPIC. Then you've found the perfect book and need to pick this up now! It's got everything in a love story you need and I'm positive it will become a favorite of yours. Samantha Towle has never disappointed me. I'm eagerly awaiting book two in this series. :)<br><br><u>
  <b>Jake and Tru</b>

</u><br><br><i>“I’ve only ever loved one girl, Tru – and that’s you. It’s always been you. I loved you from the moment I knew how to love.” ~~ Jake </i><br><br><i>“I’ll never be good enough for you, I know that. But I’m no good without you, and if that makes me a selfish bastard for wanting you as badly as I do then so be it because I can’t live a life that doesn’t have you in it.” ~~ Jake </i><br><br><i>"You're it for me. I want to be with you forever. I want you to be mine" ~~ Jake</i><br><br><br><br>P.S ~ Samantha Towle is a genius and I am a major fan.           <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48727754-chan?shelf=2020">2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48727754-chan?shelf=adult-contemporary">adult-contemporary</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2393325585" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8824461087737556816"><b>this really did not work for me.</b><br/><br/>it was mostly the writing to be honest. there was a WHOLE lot of tell and not a lot of show. we're supposed to believe that this girl was best friends with a guy, lost touch, and now he's a rock star. and she's supposed to interview him and they're gonna fall in love or whatever.<br/><br/>but we get almost NO context as to what their childhood friendship looked like. there is no relationship building in the present and we get no flashbacks to the past. we're just supposed t</span>
  <span id="freeText8824461087737556816" style="display:none"><b>this really did not work for me.</b><br /><br />it was mostly the writing to be honest. there was a WHOLE lot of tell and not a lot of show. we're supposed to believe that this girl was best friends with a guy, lost touch, and now he's a rock star. and she's supposed to interview him and they're gonna fall in love or whatever.<br /><br />but we get almost NO context as to what their childhood friendship looked like. there is no relationship building in the present and we get no flashbacks to the past. we're just supposed to believe that people with completely different aspirations and at completely different life stages are supposed to magically work because <b>we used to be best friends.</b><br /><br />it made everything feel completely unbelievable, low stakes, and pretty insta-lovey. <br /><br />this was also an issue because <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[there is a cheating plot. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> i mean i usually don't love this plot device anyway re: love triangles but it felt absolutely ridiculous that our main character would choose the rockstar she barely knows over a guy who she's actively been seeing for 2 years, GIVEN the context or lack thereof for her relationship with the rockstar.<br /><br />on top of that, our heroine, Tru(dy) was completely naive and immature in her feelings and how she handled them. if you want to be with one guy, you need to let the other guy know immediately. dragging things out doesn't spare feelings.<br /><br />had this book been written differently it could have been explosive. i like love triangles. i like rockstar romances. i like childhood best friends. but none of the pieces worked effectively here and i felt like i was reading someone's diary rather than a full fledged first person narrative.</span>

<div id="review_400315520" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/400315520" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/400315520?book_show_action=true">Aug 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=music">music</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=love-triangle">love-triangle</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer400315520" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10321908910248154020">Enjoyed this book! The writing was direct and fairly simple, but the story was engaging and I really loved the characters. The book had a sweet, fun start that slowly evolved into a more in-depth, emotional read.<br/><br/>When music journalist Trudy Bennett gets hired to interview one of the world's most famous and sexy rock stars, "Jake Wethers", she is extremely surprised and reluctant. Jake was Tru's first love. They were childhood best friends until life separated them at the age of fourteen, leaving </span>
  <span id="freeText10321908910248154020" style="display:none">Enjoyed this book! The writing was direct and fairly simple, but the story was engaging and I really loved the characters. The book had a sweet, fun start that slowly evolved into a more in-depth, emotional read.<br><br>When music journalist Trudy Bennett gets hired to interview one of the world's most famous and sexy rock stars, "Jake Wethers", she is extremely surprised and reluctant. Jake was Tru's first love. They were childhood best friends until life separated them at the age of fourteen, leaving Tru alone and heartbroken. <br><br>I don't think I need to tell you how the sexy sparks fly when these two reunite! It seems all those years apart have not diffused their connection, and a deeper attraction ignites. There is just one problem; Tru has a boyfriend, to whom she is determined on remaining faithful. Even as she agrees to go on tour with Jake and his band to cover his biography, she refuses to betray her boyfriend Will.<br><br>I cannot tell you how many times I forgot about poor Will throughout this story. I even considered trying this little 'remembering Will' tactic just so he wouldn't slip my mind again...<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/string%20on%20finger" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389005i/749933.gif" alt="Reminder Finger with String Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I'm sorry Will. You were really sweet...<br><br>I think the fact that Tru's boyfriend wasn't constantly present in this story made the love triangle pill a little easier to swallow. I sort of felt less guilty as a reader rooting for the <i>other</i> man in the absence of her current one. Speaking of guilt, I adored Tru, but I do wish her actions didn't so quickly and completely betray her thoughts. She struggled internally with the idea of hurting Will, but literally JUMPED on the first chance that arose...;) Fortunately, I was able to be more understanding when I considered the history she and Jake shared. <br><br>A steamy read with a lot of fantastic references to music. Jake was a sexy, romantic, possessive, intensely tormented hero and I fully enjoyed his journey to redemption. Looking forward to the second book of this series.<br><br><b>
  <i>"I'll never be good enough for you, I know that. But I'm no good without you, and if that makes me a selfish bastard for wanting you as badly as I do then so be it because I can't live a life that doesn't have you in it."</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> Contemporary Romance<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Maximum steam<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Complicated, extreme, and sexy.<br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Bad-boy, alpha, rocker hero. Frustrating, but strong heroine. <br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> Centers on childhood friends reuniting into an intense, passionate, but unsteady relationship. <br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Fun, smooth, and lively.<br><b>▪ POV:</b> 1st Person: Heroine <br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> None<br><b>▪	 Next Installment:</b> Follow up/Continuing story<br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">

I would look at the cover...think about starting..re-read the blurb... and then move on. After finishing the read I now know why my gut was telling me this book really wasn't for me. <br/><br/>I will get to the point... (This was one of the very few reviews I have ever ranted about)<br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[<br/>I hate cheating...   <span id="freeText3486746289915400013" style="display:none"><b>1 for Jake... but not thrilled with him either Stars-2014 Read</b><br>This book has been on my tbr list FOREVER. I would look at the cover...think about starting..re-read the blurb... and then move on. After finishing the read I now know why my gut was telling me this book really wasn't for me. <br><br>I will get to the point... (This was one of the very few reviews I have ever ranted about)<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>I hate cheating... I don't get it. I have always been of the mindset of Shit or get off the pot. If you are in a relationship, supposedly love someone for two years... then what the fuck are you doing sleeping with someone else...Tru had no excuse... there was really nothing wrong with Will. Yes... two years... no ring, no living together... whatever... but she was part of this couple. So if you start having feelings for Jake so powerful... take a moment and think... stop... Flyback if you must...break up and do it in person, then come back to Jake. But to play this game, drink to blot it out and be all "I can't tell him while banging Jake"... No...<br><br>And...Jake's not an innocent either... he knew she had someone else... so he isn't free and clear in my book either.<br><br>I hate wishy-washy women... The ones who one minute they are all in love with the guy... the next hate him... then flip like the pancake off the griddle and love him again. Tru was just plain dumb in relationships and people... to even type more about her then the cheating takes too much effort for me because there were too many moments to address...her "not wanting to be in his lifestyle"... she knows he is the most famous rocker ever.... duh...maybe she should have thought about that too... along with the cheating, hmmmm<br><br><br>So was there anything that I liked???? Well, the idea was a good one... the surprises Jake did for her were sweet..and Jake had some very cute moments but overall it was a very frustrating read. Too many things to suspend my mind and accept the behavior as ok by both characters. I understand all kinds of challenges, working them through and moving forward... but this had too many stemming from actions that work my last nerve.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>So the lesson here... is to follow your gut... because more than most of the time it is right.<br><br><strong>For more Reviews, Free E-books and Giveaways</strong><br><div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/363111530?book_show_action=true">Jul 07, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tough Critic Book Reviews" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews">Tough Critic Book Reviews</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer363111530" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer539478257201259985"><b>3.5 stars</b><br/><br/>My cherry has been popped! I am no longer a Samantha Towle virgin. This little minx is definitely someone I'd do again! I was touched in all the right places and teased with an assortment of intense emotions. <br/><br/>So if the "sex" was so good, why not more stars? Because I wasn't "turned-on" right away. The book didn't really start for me until the tour when things <i>really</i> started to happen, but then it gave it to me way too fast! The second half was so effin amazing; I definitely wanted more </span>
  <span id="freeText539478257201259985" style="display:none"><b>3.5 stars</b><br /><br />My cherry has been popped! I am no longer a Samantha Towle virgin. This little minx is definitely someone I'd do again! I was touched in all the right places and teased with an assortment of intense emotions. <br /><br />So if the "sex" was so good, why not more stars? Because I wasn't "turned-on" right away. The book didn't really start for me until the tour when things <i>really</i> started to happen, but then it gave it to me way too fast! The second half was so effin amazing; I definitely wanted more of <i>that</i>. It got so good, but then it ended way too quickly. <br /><br />Pacing issues aside though, this was a great read! WARNING: You <i>will</i> need to hydrate yourself before you read <i>The Mighty Storm</i>. You are going to sweat from the sweltering heat between Tru &amp; Jake, the physical intimacy will leave you damp and dripping, the emotional heart-ache will have you in tears!<br /><br />Nothing compares to the gut wrenching emotions a reader experiences when the hero breaks your heart. You can't breathe; it leaves you feeling physically ill! I haven't hurt like this since <i>Modern Love Story</i> or <i>The Opportunist</i>. You want to believe that Jake is prince charming, a tattooed, mischievous, and somewhat naughty prince charming; one with a really big...but still a prince charming. I hurt right along with Tru! I healed right along with Tru, I forgave right along with Tru, and I <i>came</i> right along with Tru! <br /><br />This book didn't find my "g" spot right away, but it <i>did</i> eventually find it. It found it, played with it a bit, and left me wanting more...READ ON!<br /><br />Also reviewed at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://toughcriticbookreviews.blogspot.com/">http://toughcriticbookreviews.blogspo...</a><br /></span>

<div id="review_2176428296" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2176428296" />
    <a title="Beatrice Masaluñga" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga"><img alt="Beatrice Masaluñga" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603719912p2/4590441.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2176428296?book_show_action=true">Nov 06, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beatrice Masaluñga" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beatrice Masaluñga" href="/user/show/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga">Beatrice Masaluñga</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2176428296" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3539584578220119663"><i>The Mighty Storm</i> was recommended to me by my book girlfriends. Thank you ladies 😘💕for recommending this book to me ages ago! Their raves piqued my curiosity and finally dived into my first Samantha Towle novel.<br/><br/>Music journalist <b>Trudy Bennett</b> crossed paths again with her childhood best friend and lead vocalist of a famous rock band The Mighty Storm, <b>Jake Wethers</b> as she gets a chance to exclusively interview him for the Etiquette Magazine (the company Trudy works for). They haven't seen each other </span>
  <span id="freeText3539584578220119663" style="display:none"><i>The Mighty Storm</i> was recommended to me by my book girlfriends. Thank you ladies 😘💕for recommending this book to me ages ago! Their raves piqued my curiosity and finally dived into my first Samantha Towle novel.<br /><br />Music journalist <b>Trudy Bennett</b> crossed paths again with her childhood best friend and lead vocalist of a famous rock band The Mighty Storm, <b>Jake Wethers</b> as she gets a chance to exclusively interview him for the Etiquette Magazine (the company Trudy works for). They haven't seen each other for twelve years since he migrated to United States. She's been in love with him for a longtime but at some point they lost their communication. Now that he returns in her life, the chemistry between them intensified.<br /><br /><b>What a roller coaster of events between Tru and Jake. It's full of angst, tension and scorching hot romance. </b> There are several moments I'm frustrated with Tru for all her wrong decisions and I want to shake her so badly. If only she's been honest with <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Will, who's her current boyfriend. I know she doesn't love him as much as Jake, I think she should have break up with him earlier before she had an affair with Jake. It's horrible and I feel so bad for him. He's a good man and he deserves better. *cries*  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. In fairness to her, she apologized <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[even if it's too late :( it hurts Will so bad. The dude loves her so much.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and clear things up. <br /><br /><b>As for Jake, there was more to his bad boy rock star image. </b> He had high and low points in his life. Grieving for his abusive father, drug addiction, partying and women, it came to a point of self-destruction.<b> His declaration of love with Trudy through his actions were swoon worthy.</b> He's an alpha guy who gets what he wants. He's attentive, thoughtful and very sweet to Tru. The romance between them was intimate and passionate. They are just meant to be.<br /><br />It's a great entertaining book and I enjoyed the drama. I'm looking forward to read the sequel and follow Jake and Tru's journey. I have a strong feeling I'll love it more than this book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3539584578220119663" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer406849806" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13717288696071652180">I loved the first 100 pages or so, and felt the book had promise to be great. After that, it sort of fell apart for me. There is soooooooooooooooo much unnecessary drama that could have been avoided had either of these two had stopped being self involved enough to think through their situation rationally. <br/><br/>I didn't dislike either of them, but I think I just expected a more mature relationship. This one felt like a high school love affair with adult situations and sex. <br/><br/>Basically, it wasn't a bad b</span>
  <span id="freeText13717288696071652180" style="display:none">I loved the first 100 pages or so, and felt the book had promise to be great. After that, it sort of fell apart for me. There is soooooooooooooooo much unnecessary drama that could have been avoided had either of these two had stopped being self involved enough to think through their situation rationally. <br /><br />I didn't dislike either of them, but I think I just expected a more mature relationship. This one felt like a high school love affair with adult situations and sex. <br /><br />Basically, it wasn't a bad book. The British slant of writing was kind of cool, because you don't often get a writer who won't cave in and write 'American'. I'm sure there is a technical term for it, but you get my drift. Though I'm glad I don't have to read it all of the time, because it did interrupt the flow. What is a 'vest' in the UK? Is it a tank top? I also think that there were some editing issues, but not enough for me to care all that much about.<br /><br />So for the first 100-150 pages, I give it five stars. After that, not so much. I think this is one that you really need to be in the mood for. Prepare for angst and drama, drama, drama!!! I can see the appeal, but I read it at a time that I needed something a little more toned down.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13717288696071652180" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14853212112501242515">WELL HERE IT IS !!!!!!<br/><br/>The book I have been anxiously awaiting ….THE MIGHTY STORM by SAMANTHA TOWLE !!!<br/><br/>I was a little excited when I received an advanced copy of The Mighty Storm ….ok so I was A LOT excited ………ok ok OK !!!   <span id="freeText14853212112501242515" style="display:none">WELL HERE IT IS !!!!!!<br /><br />The book I have been anxiously awaiting ….THE MIGHTY STORM by SAMANTHA TOWLE !!!<br /><br />I was a little excited when I received an advanced copy of The Mighty Storm ….ok so I was A LOT excited ………ok ok OK !!! So I may have screamed like a total girl &amp; jumped up &amp; down whilst clapping my hands ……so sue me LOL <br />Its been a while for me between Rock Star books &amp; Rock Star books are my crack !!! I for 1 was very desperate for a good fix ….OOOOHHHH BOY! DID I GET MY FIX !!!! <br /><br />OK so I don’t do “spoiler” reviews. In fact I hate spoilers in reviews but I’m going to give u as much as I can because to be honest I AM FREAKING DYING TO TALK ABOUT THIS BOOK !!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!<br /><br />This book gripped me &amp; had me emotionally invested in both the characters &amp; the story within the first few chapters. <br />Not only did I want MORE of the uber sexy tattooed rock god JAKE WETHERS…I know !! hot tattooed rock god …ummm SOLD ! RIGHT ? LOL but I also found TRUDY BENNETT (or Tru as Jake calls her ) extremely relatable , Likable &amp; an all-round awesome chick !<br />Tru is a smart, sexy music journalist. She is also the beautiful girl next door …literally!!!!<br />She grew up next door to Jake &amp; after years of being best friends she lost him when his moved with his family to America at the age of 14.  This broke Tru’s heart &amp; geeeez as a 14yr old girl all full of hormones we all know how devastated she would have been …SNIFF…oh I need chocolate just thinking about it . Anyway ….after a short time of being apart they lost contact &amp; Tru never saw or heard from Jake again .Until 12 years later when her boss Vicky landed her the interview of her career with the lead singer of 1 of the biggest rock bands in the world !!.....u gest it THE MIGHTY STORM’s JAKE WETHERS !!!!!<br /><br />INSERT GIRLY SQUEEL HERE !!!!! EEEEEEEEKKKKKKK !!!<br /><br />Now that you are a little more excited let me tell you a bit about JAKE hot-as-hell WETHERS!!!<br />Ok so u get that he is an Uber sexy tattooed rock god  we covered that already!! lol <br />Just has that larger-than-life Rock Star persona I want sooo much in a fictional character. He is a self-made success, building not only a chart topping rock band but also his own record label .He works hard but PLAYS even harder!! He likes his alcohol, drugs, cigarettes &amp; he is a habitual lady’s man…..hmmm no that’s not right…”lady’s man” sounds to tame ……let’s say he usually turns his sexy smile &amp; fuck-me eyes on a girl &amp; they drop to their knees, magically losing their panties on the way down !!!...yep that’s a better way to describe our Jake ;)<br /><br />Ok this would be the guys queue to squeal …..or grunt &amp; punch each other in the arm or whatever it is u man type people do . lol<br /><br />Jake only knows how to play to win. He is in control at all times……….until Tru that is …(“YAY TRU” I say . Score 1 for team vagina woop woop ) he has never wanted something he can’t have &amp; this frustrates Jake !! He is not use to not getting what he wants &amp;his reaction to some of those situations made me want to poke him in the eye with something pointy !!!!!<br />Now don’t get me wrong !! Jake is not all spoilt bad-boy . He is romantic &amp; warm &amp; sensitive &amp; watching him suffer broke my heart into itty bitty pieces  ..sniff sniff <br />But its not just Jake who broke me ….ohhhhhh no !!! Tru !! my poor beautiful Tru !!! see Tru has a “situation” of her own to deal with (I’m calling it the situation coz I don’t want to give too much away . I want you to experience &amp; FEEL IT like I did ) From the moment she fell back into Jakes life some might say she had a choice to make…play it safe or risk it all !!! but I believe she never had a choice . Jake is her heart <br /><br />This book has EVERYTHING a great contemporary romance needs !!<br />An unforgettable romance between two incredibly relatable characters that was beautiful. <br />There were “catch your breath” moments of angst &amp; drama that made me cry &amp; scream &amp; want to detach emotionally to save myself the pain of suffering with them . But it was impossible!!! I was in way too deep for that !! <br />There was a cast of minor characters that gave humour &amp; extra life to the story .<br />OHHHH &amp; there were what I like to call induced “1 handed reading” moments …..You know when you have to hold your kindle in 1 hand coz your other hand is busy …….you know lol…….well you get the idea. Teehee…..What I’m trying to say is the steamy “adult” scenes are hotter than a BBQ plate left in the sun on an Aussie summers day !!!!! <br />&amp; to top it off it has a hot gay man that can dance up a storm (&amp; I want him to be my BFF ) who saved me (&amp;Tru) from losing my mind &amp; stopped my hiccuppy sob fests on more than 1 occasion ……….oh bless you Stuart for being there for us !!!!<br />To say that this book affected me emotionally is a gross understatement. I found myself selfishly not wanting release day to come so I didn’t have to share Jake &amp; Tru with the rest of the world. LOL <br />Its sort of like that awkward moment when you find out that someone else thinks of your BFF as their BFF too !!!! ummmm what ?? NOOO !!! IM NOT SHARING!!! LOL I want to clutch TMS to my chest &amp; growl at anyone who comes near wanting to take a peak <br /><br />ALAS!! I must loosen my whits knuckle death grip &amp; let my baby’s go <br />&amp; my girls always say “sharing is caring Sali” lol <br /><br />So this is me letting go &amp; sharing one of the most wonderful books I have read !!!<br /><br />ENJOY ALL MY BOOK WHORE AWESOME MATES OUT THERE !!!!<br /><br />ROCK ON BITCHES !!!!<br /><br />OWWW 1 MORE THING !!!!........MAKE SURE U DON’T MISS THE SPECIAL LITTLE BONUS AT THE END !!!!! ITS FUCKING AWESOME <br />&amp; if u really want to get the most out of this awesome new release come over to TOTALLYBOOKED Facebook page on release day Friday 24th of August. We are doing a big group read of THE MIGHTY STORM !!! It’s an amazing way to share your reading experience with other like-minded readers . There will also be lots of other special surprises posted about the book &amp; the talented Author SAMMANTHA TOWLE . Sam will also be there to chat with her  <br />Looking forward to seeing u all there <br /><br />Oh, and another thing...sorry, I'll finish in a minute. I've noticed a couple of comments on here referring to this book as being "just like Thoughtless" and I want to make a call on that right now. It isn't ! <br />It has Jake, lead singer of a band and a love triangle and that's where the similarities end! This book is totally different in feel and execution. Read it and see for yourself!<br /><br />LOL OK I PROMISE IM DONE NOW :).......now go get ready for a read-a-thon party with us on friday !!!!<br /></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3895224658497600328">I liked this book a lot. Unfortunately I couldn't give it five stars because of the editing issues. The grammatical and spelling errors were atrocious. Ms. Towle needs a new editor.<br/><br/>That being said, I loved everything else about this book. Jake and Tru were meant to be together. Tru was a annoying at first, but I liked her by the end. Jake, well come on, what's not to like about him. I'm a sucker for tattooed bad boys with a good heart, and that's Jake. The last concert scene when Jake sang "Hurt</span>
  <span id="freeText3895224658497600328" style="display:none">I liked this book a lot. Unfortunately I couldn't give it five stars because of the editing issues. The grammatical and spelling errors were atrocious. Ms. Towle needs a new editor.<br /><br />That being said, I loved everything else about this book. Jake and Tru were meant to be together. Tru was a annoying at first, but I liked her by the end. Jake, well come on, what's not to like about him. I'm a sucker for tattooed bad boys with a good heart, and that's Jake. The last concert scene when Jake sang "Hurt" to Tru melted me completely. I love that song, both versions, and it was so appropriate at that point in the story. <br /><br />If your still on the fence about reading this because of the infidelity issue, all I can say is it's an important part of the story, but it's not just about that. We read romance books and unfortunately in romantic relationships people do cheat. I think this book handles that issue well. <br /><br />So all and all I'm glad I decided to read this. I think a second book about Simone and Denny would be great! <br /><br />(Thanks Jo for telling me I'll love it. You were right! )<br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_399529726" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/399529726" />
    <a title="Lindsay" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5206569-lindsay"><img alt="Lindsay" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1477524546p2/5206569.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/399529726?book_show_action=true">Aug 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lindsay" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lindsay" href="/user/show/5206569-lindsay">Lindsay</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Anyone who loves emotion, angst and rock stars</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5206569-lindsay?shelf=on-blog">on-blog</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5206569-lindsay?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5206569-lindsay?shelf=reviews">reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5206569-lindsay?shelf=musicians-rock-star">musicians-rock-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5206569-lindsay?shelf=bad-boy-heroes">bad-boy-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5206569-lindsay?shelf=past-together">past-together</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer399529726" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15486376736334513762">This book left me with a smile on my face. I absolutely loved it. From page one I was sucked into the drama of Jake and Tru and I couldn’t stop reading. I was obsessed. I was thinking about it while at work, wishing it was excruciatingly slow so that I could read. <br/><br/>Jake Wethers is a guy with issues. After dealing with the death of a close friend he goes off the rails and into rehab. He is screwed up and he makes for a great read. He’s a recovering addict, party boy, playboy but he loves Tru above</span>
  <span id="freeText15486376736334513762" style="display:none">This book left me with a smile on my face. I absolutely loved it. From page one I was sucked into the drama of Jake and Tru and I couldn’t stop reading. I was obsessed. I was thinking about it while at work, wishing it was excruciatingly slow so that I could read. <br><br>Jake Wethers is a guy with issues. After dealing with the death of a close friend he goes off the rails and into rehab. He is screwed up and he makes for a great read. He’s a recovering addict, party boy, playboy but he loves Tru above all else and that shows. <br><br>I loved the relationship between Tru and Jake. They had been childhood best friends and lost touch after Jake’s family moved away. They reconnect in the beginning of the book and find out that both had had crushes on the other when they were teenagers. The connection was instant and the history between the two really shined through. <br><br>Music played a huge part in this book. Both Jake and Tru grew up on music at the hand of her father. Music was instrumental to them. It defined their lives. Since I also grew up that way, I could relate to that. There was a particular passage that brought tears to my eyes just for its meaning alone: <br><br> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“If you, Jake Wethers, had to pick one song as your title song to describe yourself, what would it be – and it can’t be one of your own,” I quickly add.<br>	“Hurt,” he answers without hesitation. <br>	It makes me hurt inside he picked that song.<br>	“Why?”<br>	He lets out a light sigh. “Some people said Reznor was writing a lyrical suicide note, others said he was writing about finding a reason to live. I think it’s both…it just depends on which side you’re looking at it from.” <br>	“And which side are you looking at it from?”<br>	He stares at me from a long moment. My heart is hammering in my chest.<br>	“Now? …a reason to live.”<br>	My insides start to tremble. <br>	“Reznor’s version or Johnny Cash’s?” I ask quietly, trying to conceal the pain from my voice.<br>	“Johnny Cash.”<br>	“Why?”<br>	He closes his eyes briefly. And in this moment I just want to magic up all the power in the world to soothe his pains away.<br>	“Because I have a few things in common with him,” he answers, opening his eyes.<br>	“Like?”<br>	“The drugs…the women…hanging out for the girl of my dreams.”<br>	I take a sharp breath in. tears instantly prick the backs of my eyes.<br>	He touches my face, his thumb smoothing over my lips. “You’re my June, Tru.”<br>	</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>	<br>That same passage comes back at the end of the book when Jake switches the song from Cash’s version to Reznor’s. It left me blinking back tears. Here are links to both versions so you get an idea of the differences:<br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=SmVAWKfJ4Go" rel="nofollow noopener">Johnny Cash's "Hurt"</a> <br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=OKdEYxtH_k4" rel="nofollow noopener">Trent Reznor's "Hurt"</a><br><br>Just listening to the differences in the songs is enough to make me tear up for Jake. The end was perfect for this couple and this book. Music was what reconnected them in the beginning of the book, so it was perfectly fitting that music would mend the rift between them. When nothing else would show Tru exactly what Jake was feeling, Reznor’s song got through to her. <br><br>Another song that Jake sings in the book is Wicked Game by Chris Isaak. A really great version that is perfect for Jake is by <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=JIvTUXbgbqU" rel="nofollow noopener">Three Days Grace.</a> <br><br>This book has definitely earned a place on my “favorites” shelf and I will absolutely be re-reading it. And since the author recently announced that there will be a sequel, I'll be anxiously waiting for it. <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[And if you’re interested in band photos: <br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>Jake:<br><a href="http://s1158.photobucket.com/albums/p608/LWolf5/Goodreads%20Guys/TMS/?action=view&amp;current=Jake-BoRoberts.png" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388881i/749710.png" alt="Jake" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br>Denny:<br><a href="http://s1158.photobucket.com/albums/p608/LWolf5/Goodreads%20Guys/TMS/?action=view&amp;current=Denny-SamuelTrepanier.png" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img <div id="review_362973609" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/362973609" />
    <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog"><img alt="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554795448p2/3870376.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/362973609?book_show_action=true">Jul 07, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog">Jenny - TotallybookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer362973609" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7102359356772941746">Review also at: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://totallybookedblog.com/'>http://totallybookedblog.com/</a><br/><br/>I was given the most amazing opportunity to Beta read this book. <br/><br/>Where to start with The Mighty Storm?? First off, I loved this book. I mean, I really loved this book! 5 star read for me without a doubt!<br/><br/>Really,what’s not to love? There’s a hot, can’t be tamed, tattooed bad boy rock god named Jake Wethers…….(heart palpitations here – get me a defibrillator stat!!) for starters!<br/><br/>Not only that, it’s got romance, angst, drama, emotion, humour, music refere</span>
  <span id="freeText7102359356772941746" style="display:none">Review also at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://totallybookedblog.com/">http://totallybookedblog.com/</a><br /><br />I was given the most amazing opportunity to Beta read this book. <br /><br />Where to start with The Mighty Storm?? First off, I loved this book. I mean, I really loved this book! 5 star read for me without a doubt!<br /><br />Really,what’s not to love? There’s a hot, can’t be tamed, tattooed bad boy rock god named Jake Wethers…….(heart palpitations here – get me a defibrillator stat!!) for starters!<br /><br />Not only that, it’s got romance, angst, drama, emotion, humour, music references, hot sex and oh did I mention hot, tattooed bad boy rock star Jake Wethers???<br /><br />Now that I’ve got that out the way, let’s get serious.<br /><br />This book wasn’t just about “gorgeous as all hell” Jake, although he was certainly a very pleasant part of the book .<br /><br />The story is told through Tru’s (Trudy Bennett) eyes and centres on her and her former best friend Jake finding each other after twelve years apart and realising they still have feelings they thought were long buried.<br /><br />You will feel for Tru as she discovers feelings for Jake she knows she shouldn’t have. He’s her former best friend, yes, she loved him as a teenager and he broke her heart when he left her at fourteen, but Tru has moved on. She is in love with Will, her wonderful boyfriend of two years and she must hold onto that relationship, whilst at the same time try to deny and conceal the feelings she has for Jake.<br /><br />Jake (lead singer of The Mighty Storm) is dealing with past demons and Tru coming into his life gives him a purpose he didn’t know he needed until she returned.<br /><br />In Jake, the author has managed to bring us a strong, alpha, hot, yet sensitive and loving male lead character who is humanly flawed and let me tell you ladies, this guy is going to be the stuff of women’s fantasies that’s for sure!<br /><br />But not only has she managed to bring to life such wonderful characters in Tru and Jake, but also the supporting characters of the band, Denny, Tom, Smith and of course Jake’s PA Stuart who I just adored.<br /><br />This book had it all for me. It was a book about human relationships, human eff ups, human frailties and of course the world of a high profile rock star who tries to find a life of normality in a world of abnormality for himself and Tru.<br /><br />Jake is a man who always gets what he wants, but will Tru be the one thing he can’t have?<br /><br />I enjoyed every minute of this book, though I have to say, be prepared, because there were times that I actually clutched my chest and cried, such is the truthfulness of the writing in some of the scenes which you will discover throughout the book.<br />This is Samantha Towle’s first foray into the contemporary romance genre and wow! Did she nail it!<br /><br />What I like about Samantha’s writing here is that she explores the little nuances of her characters that allows the reader the ability to feel like you’re actually part of this story . Allows you to be a part of the world that is Jake, Tru and The Mighty Storm. You will feel like you’re really there with them, in the room and living this story through Tru’s eyes.<br /><br />I love nothing more than finding a book that has the ability to draw me in and hold me there until the very last page. A book where I can feel what the characters feel and see what the characters see. It makes me feel a part of something and enables me to “live” the book rather just ” read” a story and that’s exactly how I felt experiencing The Mighty Storm.<br /><br />I’m not going to go into details about the story because to give anything away would be an injustice to other readers and I want them to experience this book as I did. To experience it the way the author intended it to be read.<br /><br />Yes readers…….. freeze some dinners, hold the housework, tell the family to fend for themselves because once you start reading The Mighty Storm, you are not going to want to put it down!<br /><br />Be sure to keep reading and click past the end because there a little “bonus” at the back you won’t want to miss!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7102359356772941746" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
