    <a title="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14351108-deanna-pink-lady"><img alt="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1370640721p2/14351108.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/599152943?book_show_action=true">Apr 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️" href="/user/show/14351108-deanna-pink-lady">Deanna❤Pink Lady❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14351108-deanna-pink-lady?shelf=my-vault">my-vault</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer599152943" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3966953748893201613"><b>5 "First Love" Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/da774cc6b7833100ce5dac80c42d1700_zps7e580f8d.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418938i/829957._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo da774cc6b7833100ce5dac80c42d1700_zps7e580f8d.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Jake Wethers lived next door to Trudy Bennett while growing up in England. Everything changed when he moved to America with his family at the age of 14. They kept up with each other for a while but eventually the letters stopped and so did the phone calls. Life goes on, you live your life, but do you ever forget? Young Love, First Love, True Love, Love Not Forgotten.....Can 12 years of not seeing each other bring back those feelings or has time erased what might have been</span>
  <span id="freeText3966953748893201613" style="display:none"><b>5 "First Love" Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/da774cc6b7833100ce5dac80c42d1700_zps7e580f8d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418938i/829957._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo da774cc6b7833100ce5dac80c42d1700_zps7e580f8d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Jake Wethers lived next door to Trudy Bennett while growing up in England. Everything changed when he moved to America with his family at the age of 14. They kept up with each other for a while but eventually the letters stopped and so did the phone calls. Life goes on, you live your life, but do you ever forget? Young Love, First Love, True Love, Love Not Forgotten.....Can 12 years of not seeing each other bring back those feelings or has time erased what might have been?<br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Tru_zps6a9371bd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418938i/829958._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Tru_zps6a9371bd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Jake_zpsb0a06a05.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418938i/829959._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Jake_zpsb0a06a05.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After 12 yrs, Trudy is going to interview Jake for her magazine. Will he remember her, will he even recognize her, she is nervous and not sure what to expect..<br><br><b>My eyes meet his, and I see it....the instant recognition. He remembers me. <br><br>"Trudy Bennett?" he repeats. "My Trudy Bennett?" His Trudy Bennett?<br><br>And seeing Jake, looking like this, I just know that I am so completely and totally fucked. Because I'm now fourteen year old Trudy all over again.</b><br><br>So the story begins and what a story it is. It is a wonderful, beautiful, angsty, frustrating, maddening, heartbreaking, swooning love story. I read this book in one day, I just couldn't put it down and well when you have a hot, gorgeous rock star who has a down and dirty side, who reconnects with the love of his life, could you put that down? This story is about Jake and Tru and their discovery of the love that each had for each other so many years ago and how that love is still present. The one big complication is that Tru has a boyfriend. Gorgeous, loving, stable Will, boyfriend of 2 years, loves Trudy completely and would do anything for her. Then there is Jake, rock star, womanizer, drug addict and the love of her life.....<br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Couples/tumblr_lr183yLnp51qbkl8s_zps878bb80a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413543ra/814424.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_lr183yLnp51qbkl8s_zps878bb80a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/Truandjake_zps03aec26f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418938i/829960._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Truandjake_zps03aec26f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/image_zpsf963569e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406907i/794337.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpsf963569e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/tms3_zps866c477e.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418938i/829961._SY540_.png" alt=" photo tms3_zps866c477e.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>This story pulls out all your emotions. Tru was frustrating but I understood her reasoning sometimes and other times I wanted to slap her silly. Jake on the other hand stole my heart. He has his demons and works at keeping them at bay, not always successful, but the one thing that grounds him is Tru. His expression of love for her throughout the book had me swooning, sighing and wishing against all hope that my name was Tru.<br><br>Some of my favorite and beautiful Jake quotes:<b><br>"I love you," he repeats. "I've only ever loved one girl, Tru- and that's you. It's always been you. I loved you from the moment I knew how to love."<br><br>"You're it for me. I want to be with you forever. I want you to be mine."<br><br>It's a love/hate relationship, baby. I love how they look on you. Hate that they're blocking my access."<br><br>When I said you looked well, what I really should have said was that you look beautiful.x<br><br>"Johnny Cash...I have a few things in common with him."<br>"Like?"<br>"The drugs...the women...hanging out for the girl of my dreams...you're my June, Tru."<br><br>"I'm nothing without you Tru, nothing."<br><br>"I'll never be good enough for you, I know that. But I'm no good without you, and if that makes me a selfish bastard for wanting you as badly as I do then so be it because I can't live a life that doesn't have you in it."</b><br><br><a href="http://s1333.photobucket.com/user/Dpbarton/media/a2339db60d948b9d2321114828cabe56_zps3385c535.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380418938i/829962._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo a2339db60d948b9d2321114828cabe56_zps3385c535.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>I see that Jake is my mighty storm. He's broken and complex, and no one knows him like I do, or ever will. He needs me. He's my storm to calm. And I'm going to spend the rest of my life doing just that.</b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes, I'll marry you. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br>I must thank my fabulous Pinkies Barb and Jxxx for making me read this book so that I could join them on the BR of Wethering the Storm. I really had no idea what to expect. I was reassured that I would love it and to jump in...and ladies.......<b> I LOVED IT!!!!!</b> You both know me so well♥♥♥<br><br>PS- Wethering the Storm is fanfreakingtastic <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[but bring on the Kleenex cause it's one hell of a ride!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_403529853" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/403529853" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/403529853?book_show_action=true">Aug 30, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=super-rich-hero">super-rich-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=smuttastic">smuttastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=tattooed-hero">tattooed-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=cover-lust-i-has-it">cover-lust-i-has-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=shy-heroine">shy-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=scarred-heroes">scarred-heroes</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer403529853" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16423804420522504804"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389516i/750629._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo WETFORWETHERSXXX_zps2cc94c71.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>OK, so I know what you’re all going to say. This book was released about eight months ago so what am I doing only reading it now. Well, you know how it is. There’s always so many good books that you want to read and never enough time to read them all and this is one of those that I managed to miss but I always regretted it, always wanted to go back and read it and, just recently, Jake Wethers was mentioned in passing in another book and I just had to go back and find him again and I’m so glad I </span>
  <span id="freeText16423804420522504804" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389516i/750629._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo WETFORWETHERSXXX_zps2cc94c71.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>OK, so I know what you’re all going to say. This book was released about eight months ago so what am I doing only reading it now. Well, you know how it is. There’s always so many good books that you want to read and never enough time to read them all and this is one of those that I managed to miss but I always regretted it, always wanted to go back and read it and, just recently, Jake Wethers was mentioned in passing in another book and I just had to go back and find him again and I’m so glad I did. To think, he’s been waiting patiently on my Kindle for all these months!!<br><br>I do love me a troubled, bad boy hero and a troubled bad boy hero is exactly what I found in Jake Wethers. He’s lived the hedonistic life of a mega-famous rock-star – drink, drugs, easy women but he’s never really found true happiness. He’s never forgotten Tru, the girl he grew up with, his next door neighbour and the only girl he has ever loved. They’ve lost touch over the years but fate is about to throw them back together and launch them on an incredible emotional roller-coaster of a journey that held my attention rapt from beginning to end.<br><br>Jake is the archetypal rock star – he’s lean, muscular, tattooed and totally gorgeous. Tru is completely mesmerised by his presence – he’s sexy, he’s beautiful and he’s flirting outrageously with her. He’s got a whole heck of a lot of demons in his past that have fuelled his addictions – blissful oblivion being just another line of coke away but he’s trying to clean up his act and, now that Tru is back in his life, he’s got a reason to live again. He’s got a heart of gold and is incredibly generous and sweet despite his bad boy persona but he’s kind of moody, has a real short fuse and how MUCH did I freaking adore him? *melts* He compares himself to Johnny Cash singing Hurt and I positively melted when he tells True that she’s his June.<br><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Johnny Cash … I have a few things in common with him.”<br><br>“Like?”<br><br>“The drugs … the women … hanging out for the girl of my dreams … you’re my June, Tru.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br><br>Tru is a great heroine, very much the regular girl about town we all are. I love it when the girl next door type in a book manages to attract the attention of someone like Jake – he’s pretty much the most famous rock God on the planet and yet he’s got eyes only for Tru. Story lines like this just fill me with hope and make me smile.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>I’m so totally mesmerised by him.<br><br>And so totally in lust with him.<br><br>And so totally screwed.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Of course, both of them are fairly flawed characters and make several mistakes and they both hurt each other badly during the course of the story but then that’s real life right? We all make mistakes and we all deal with the guilt. Tru has a boyfriend, Will, at the beginning of the story and he gets hurt pretty badly by Tru &amp; Jake, both physically and emotionally and my heart hurt a lot for him. I understand that there was no way around hurting him but I felt very sorry for him.<br><br>Most of all though, I think I loved the way that Jake completely adored Tru, how deeply he loved her. He’s never been able to replicate those feelings he had for her all those years ago and the only person that ever came close, drove his car into a ravine leaving Jake in a terrible depression. She’s all he’s ever wanted.<br><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>You ask what I want from you?” His eyes move to my lips, then my eyes. “I want you, Tru. I just want you. All day, every day.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>*wibble*<br><br>There’s a totally beautiful scene at Lumb Falls in the Yorkshire Dales – this is such a gorgeous part of England.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389516i/750630._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo lumbfalls_zps24fd9973.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><br>So Tru &amp; Jake take us on a breath-taking journey, full of peaks and troughs, highs and lows, incredible happiness and intense misery. It’s a fantastic story and I just could not put this book down. It consumed my thoughts all day when I couldn’t be reading and I was constantly on edge, desperate to get back to it. It’s a real yo-yo romance, they’re happy one minute and hissing at each other like a pair of alley-cats the next. I never knew what was coming next and I was constantly on tenterhooks, just desperate for them to find that happiness they both deserved.<br><br>4.5 sexy stars<br><br>Roll on the sequel!<br><br><i>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a> or visit us on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/sinfullysexybookreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="16423804420522504804" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_362994542" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/362994542" />
    <a title="Lisa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8179357-lisa"><img alt="Lisa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1346526379p2/8179357.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/362994542?book_show_action=true">Jul 07, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa" href="/user/show/8179357-lisa">Lisa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8179357-lisa?shelf=loved">loved</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8179357-lisa?shelf=indie">indie</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer362994542" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11169336973999545706">The Mighty Storm was a completely invigorating, mindblowing ride on the Angst Express! I am an angst addict and get really crabby when I don’t read something angsty for awhile. Let’s just say I should be happy for days and days!<br/><br/>The Mighty Storm is my first Samantha Towle experience and it will not be my last. When I read a great, angst filled romance, my heart beats faster and I can feel every little twist and turn in the relationship in my chest. This book had me all in a flutter, a flutter tha</span>
  <span id="freeText11169336973999545706" style="display:none">The Mighty Storm was a completely invigorating, mindblowing ride on the Angst Express! I am an angst addict and get really crabby when I don’t read something angsty for awhile. Let’s just say I should be happy for days and days!<br /><br />The Mighty Storm is my first Samantha Towle experience and it will not be my last. When I read a great, angst filled romance, my heart beats faster and I can feel every little twist and turn in the relationship in my chest. This book had me all in a flutter, a flutter that I haven’t quite felt since I first read some of my favorites like The Opportunist, Thoughtless and Love Unscripted. Angst is like dessert to me; I need it, I crave it, and I love it. This particular book was a delectible chocolate cupcake with cream cheese filling and chocolate ganache on top (the book mentioned French pastries and I can’t get them out of my mind now!).<br /><br />So get on the Angst Express with me here for a minute; I want to explain exactly what kind of trip you are going to get if you hop on board. At first it is smooth, taking in the view and getting to know the layout. Then, there is an uphill journey that brings you to the top of highest mountain where the view is breathtaking and quite frankly you never want to come down. But what is the old saying? What goes up must come down? The same is true of the Angst Express and it shoots up and down a few times going so fast that your heart is beating out of your chest and you have trouble catching your breath. As the ride continues and comes to as end, you will hope the whole ride was worth the highs and lows, twists and turns. IT.IS.SO.FREAKING.WORTH.IT!<br /><br />Tru is one of those female characters that will get on some readers nerves, I am not going to lie. She has a great boyfriend who loves and adores her but he isn’t her first love and soulmate. Yes, she loves him but it is not THAT love. Tru is indecisive at times, trying to figure out what she wants and whether or not she should put herself first. She doesn’t always think she is deserving of the good things that come her way and doesn’t always see what others see in her. She is strong even though she is indecisive; she isn’t anyones stepping stone and will stick up for herself if need be. I really actually liked Tru because I would be a hypocrite not to. There are other books where I want the soulmates to be together no matter what and I can’t hold it against Tru that she was dating a great guy when she found her soulmate again. It would be really hard to be in that situation!<br /><br />Jake is troubled, broken, sexy, sweet and just about everything I love in a male character. Oh, and he is a rockstar! Most of all, I love the way he loves Tru. Yes, he does have a few relationship faults but the poor guy has never been in a relationship so he is learning everything as he begins with Tru. Life with a troubled rockstar isn’t always easy; he has a temper, can be a bit irrational and has some skeletons to work through. He did some things that made me want to shake and curse him but in the end, Jake is extremely hard not to love! He had my heart the moment he took Tru to Pizza Hut:)<br /><br />Is love enough? That is a question that often went through my head while reading this. Tru and Jake have such a connection that started when they were very young but there are demons in their past that must be overcome. Their love is like my favorite football team; I root for them in good times and bad and I would be a fan no matter what happens. Relationships that start with solid friendships are always my favorite;)<br /><br />I liked Will, Tru’s boyfriend, and hated that he may get his heart broken in all this but I am thinking that he would be great in a book of his own;) I feel the same way about Tom; he could start my heart on fire if he had a book of his own. I love when books give me so many characters to love and think about for days to come!<br /><br />The Mighty Storm is an overall FANTASTIC reading experience full of romance, drama, angst, real-life issues and everything in between. I highly recommend to….well everyone!<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11169336973999545706" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText10028935010505468426" style="display:none"><br><b>** 4 I ♥ Jake but can't f*cking stand Tru stars **</b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=24l4my8" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

Jake makes up for most of Tru's shortcomings and makes Kellan look like one GIANT pussy that he is! All in all, this was an entertaining read. <br><br>If you <i>love</i> your rock star bad boys &amp; <i>hate</i> women they end up with, this book is for you.<br><br>Cheers!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10781688248292823699"><b>MADRE MIA DE MI VIDAAAAAAA!!!</b> I loved this book!<br/><br/><b>***SPOILERS AHEAD CHICAS***</b><br/><br/>Yes Jake, I am spanish, I have a funny accent and I can talk in spanish to you ALLL THE TIME, lol... Just saying, just in case this thing with Tru is not working... you know :)<br/><br/>Well, I am gonna try to be serious now... This is my first review with pics (thanks Candace), so I am sooooo excited!!! <br/><br/>I bought this book AGES ago and I want to kill myself for taking sooo long to read it!<br/><br/>First of all, they are Brits, I mean, do I </span>
  <span id="freeText10781688248292823699" style="display:none"><b>MADRE MIA DE MI VIDAAAAAAA!!!</b> I loved this book!<br><br><b>***SPOILERS AHEAD CHICAS***</b><br><br>Yes Jake, I am spanish, I have a funny accent and I can talk in spanish to you ALLL THE TIME, lol... Just saying, just in case this thing with Tru is not working... you know :)<br><br>Well, I am gonna try to be serious now... This is my first review with pics (thanks Candace), so I am sooooo excited!!! <br><br>I bought this book AGES ago and I want to kill myself for taking sooo long to read it!<br><br>First of all, they are Brits, I mean, do I need any other reason to read a book? I am not even gonna answer that. She lives in Camden for fucks sake, one of my favorites place in the UK (well, I love Richmond also but come on! Camden is A.M.A.Z.I.N.G). I have said this a million times but I have been living in the UK for 2 years so I love that country and it is amazing when you read about a place in a book and you imagine the place but it is even more amazing when you have been in that place. The first time I went to London on holidays was in May 2003 and I went to that fucking Pizza Hut in Camden, the one with the stairs!!! OMGGGGGG :)<br><br>I am not really into famous people books if you know what I mean, I feel a little bit like Tru about that, I don't think it's easy having a relationship with someone so famous, that's why I didn't read this one earlier but I was wrong! <br><br>Tru and Jake have been friends since they were little, they were in love with each other but nothing happened and then Jake leaves the UK to go to America with his mum and they don't see each other in 12 years. After 12 years he is super famous and True is a musical journalist and she has to interview him. <br>She has a boyfriend, a lovely english man called Will who is soooo in love with her (Will if you read this pls PM your phone number and I will call you the next time I am going to London, I promise).<br><br>I like the plot, no scrap that, I LOVE THE PLOT. I know most of the people here are not into cheating and I am not saying I support cheating but sometimes it happens and it is obvious that they have been in love since forever so when Jake offers her to go on tour with them you know something is gonna happen.<br><br>So the tour starts... and the unavoidable happens. And I understand Tru, she is in love with him even if she cares for Will. Come one guys, judging her is the easy thing to do.<br><br>The last day of the tour Will turns up in the hotel with Simone (I love best friends like her) and the drama starts. Jake wants Tru to tell Will but that is not easy! She cares for Will, she can't say "hey, I have been sleeping with him, laters!"... It is not that easy sooo Jake goes mad, kisses a girl and lots of great things happen. That <b> Mr Brightside moment </b>!!! O.M.G. Joderrrrrrrrrr!!!! This is Jake in that moment:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398656i/770701._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I think that is my favorite part of the book. I though everything was going to be boring from now on but I was sooooo wrong as the book didn't lose the intensity. I loved every single problem they had and I loved the way they love each other. <br><br>And the end of the book, I mean, Jake's POV??? Many thanks for that part, I loved it, I knew he was checking her ass the first time he saw her, I knew it!!! LOL<br><br><span>[image error]</span><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398656i/770702._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">"/&gt;<br><br>My favorite parts of the book (including quotes):<br><br>*She loves Adele, we are soul mates :)<br><br><i>Now would be fine with me. Yesterday, whenever, I'm easy</i><br><br>*Their moment having french cakes, awwwwwww he is sooo romantic!<br><br>*Their moment in Arola! Sergi Arola is one of the best chefs in the world! And he is spanish, yeahhhh. And this is the restaurant in Barcelona:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398656i/770703.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>He looks up at my approach and the second my eyes meet with his, whatever sense I had just talked myself into, packs its bags and fucks off, leaving me to the mercy of my hormones</i><br><br>"I start a job. I finish it" Hell yeah, you are hot Jake!<br><br>"Who was she?"<br>"No one... someone who should have been you" TOMA YA!<br><br><i>I'm going to Hell. Straight to Hell</i><br><br><i>Why isn't he straight?<br>Actually no, my life is complicated enough as it is without trying to add another guy into the picture</i><br><br>"Because it's healthy to spend time apart"<br>"That's just Cosmo bullshit."<br><br>*Their Lumb Falls moment:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398656i/770704._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*The new phone with Lumb Falls pic and the exclusive a capella song from Adele, OMG!<br><br><b>When I said you looked well, what I really should have said was that you look beautiful. x </b><br><br>*Jake wears Converse! I love Converse, I love a guy in Converse, there is nothing sexier... well yeah, a barefoot guy is sexier :)<br><br>"I'll never be good enough for you, I know that. But I'm no good without you, and if that makes me a selfish bastard for wanting you as badly as I do then so be it because I can't live a life that doesn't have you in it"<br><br>I LOVED JAKE'S POV:<br><br><i>Of course it's her you fuckwit</i><br>"Shit, it really is you"<br><i>What the hell is wrong with me? Why can't I stop talking like a dumbass?<i><br><br><i>Stuart and a dude. Stuart and a dude</i><br><br><i>What's the point in sitting on shit trying to figure it out for yourself when the answer to your question is sitting right in front of you</i><br><br>"Stuart, I need your gay-pertise"<br><br><b>BIEN HECHO SAMANTHA :)</b><br><br><br><br><br><br><br></i></i></span>

<div id="review_400008482" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/400008482" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/400008482?book_show_action=true">Aug 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer400008482" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7780399448294788048">**4.5 stars**<br/><br/>Trudy Bennett is a music journalist working for Etiquette magazine and has to interview the lead singer for the hugely successful band, The Mighty Storm. The problem is that she used to be best friends...and secretly in love with the lead singer until they fell out of contact twelve years ago. <br/><br/>I really enjoy the childhood friends turn lovers plot and this did not disappoint. Trudy, aka Tru, is a bit freaked out about Jake which is understandable. He is in a whole other universe and </span>
  <span id="freeText7780399448294788048" style="display:none">**4.5 stars**<br /><br />Trudy Bennett is a music journalist working for Etiquette magazine and has to interview the lead singer for the hugely successful band, The Mighty Storm. The problem is that she used to be best friends...and secretly in love with the lead singer until they fell out of contact twelve years ago. <br /><br />I really enjoy the childhood friends turn lovers plot and this did not disappoint. Trudy, aka Tru, is a bit freaked out about Jake which is understandable. He is in a whole other universe and is a known womanizer so she is constantly battling her feelings over the logical thing to do. Plus she has a boyfriend...a really sweet and wonderful boyfriend. <br /><br />The beginning is pretty slow...and wordy!! I think that's about the only thing that I didn't care for but it does get better. There are also a lot of British terms in the book which may (or may not) be confusing for some American readers.<br /><br />I did enjoy Tru even with all her inner turmoils! I could really sympathize and I just found it endearing. I do wish she would've handled things with Will a bit differently. <br /><br />Jake is amazing, of course, but what made him amazing was his faults. He very much goes after what he wants and damn the consequences. He does everything, and I mean everything, to the extreme whether it's good or bad and the bad is heart wrenching. I was surprised about Jake after his Dad died...I really didn't think he would do that.<br /><br />Tru's best friend and roommate, Simone, is wonderful but I wish we would have gotten more of her. I liked how she was there for Tru and it was great what happened with her. <br /><br />All the members of the band, security, etc., were great as well. They all have interesting personalities and really add to the story but I love Stuart. He really shined in the story and I would love to get to know more about him.<br /><br />Poor Will...what happens with him broke my heart. And especially when he met up with Tru later. I really wish there would have been "something" to show things would be better for him. <br /><br />I LOVED all the drama even with what happened with Will. But I LOVED the part towards the end better. OMG when Tru walked into the bedroom, I about died!! Sooo emotionally heart breaking and I LOVED not knowing how it would end!! I really wasn't sure if they would make it or not. <br /><br />There are many good smexy parts although not extremely detailed but it is sooo romantic that I didn't really mind. And what is it about these guys being so huge?? Every single book...I kid you not! <br /><br />The ending was fantastic although a bit clique and you just knew the pink "thing" WOULD happen. Plus we get the first chapter of the book from Jake's POV in Meet Jake. It made me laugh to see how vulnerable he was. Happily, I found out that the author is working on the next book and it will have some more parts with Jake's POV and it will be out in Spring 2013. I just love when they do that! <br /><br />Here's also a link for a great trailer for the book:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?feature=player_embedded&amp;v=RNKJFU6A0yg">http://www.youtube.com/watch?feature=...</a><br /><br /><br />I would definitely recommend it if you like all that emotional drama and childhood friends turned lovers. Just give yourself time to get past the beginning and you won't be disappointed! <br /><br />Oh and before I forget...don't you love the cover?? ~ Sigh ~ <br /><br /><br />Favorite quotes: <br /><br />♥ “I’ve only ever loved one girl, Tru – and that’s you. It’s <i>always</i> been you. I loved you from the moment I knew how to love.”<br /><br />♥ “I love that it’s our thing … so do you want me to put them back on so you can rip them off?”<br /><br />♥ “And that’s why I prefer to dance in the bedroom.”<br /><br />♥ My best friend. My lover. My life.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7780399448294788048" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_400671986" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/400671986" />
    <a title="Spoiler Whore-Momoa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3531683-spoiler-whore-momoa"><img alt="Spoiler Whore-Momoa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557708088p2/3531683.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/400671986?book_show_action=true">Aug 26, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Spoiler Whore-Momoa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Spoiler Whore-Momoa" href="/user/show/3531683-spoiler-whore-momoa">Spoiler Whore-Momoa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer400671986" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9693307996785759218">This is one of the reasons I love to read. I love to get sucked into a story, love to put myself in a heroine's position, go thru the emotions of said heroine and come out with a HEA. Especially if the hero is from a childhood/teenage crush.<br/><br/>Trudy Bennett is given the opportunity to interview Jake Wethers, lead singer to The Mighty Storm, her former BF and childhood crush. She works as a columnist for a magazine in the UK where she and Jake were once neighbors until he moved to the US. Jake Wethe</span>
  <span id="freeText9693307996785759218" style="display:none">This is one of the reasons I love to read. I love to get sucked into a story, love to put myself in a heroine's position, go thru the emotions of said heroine and come out with a HEA. Especially if the hero is from a childhood/teenage crush.<br /><br />Trudy Bennett is given the opportunity to interview Jake Wethers, lead singer to The Mighty Storm, her former BF and childhood crush. She works as a columnist for a magazine in the UK where she and Jake were once neighbors until he moved to the US. Jake Wethers has come out of rehab after spiraling out of control due to drugs and if you really think about it, the death of his great friend/bandmate Jonny. She is completely nervous about seeing him again after 12 years thinking he might not remember her but in Meet Jake, we know he has never forgotten Tru. After interview he asks her out for dinner for a trip down memory lane.<br /><br />What I loved about this is how easily they pick up after so many years apart. The reminiscing, flirting and the slight bantering. Tru starts feeling bad because she knows the love for Jake has never really left while she's with her boyfriend Will. The next day when she goes back to work she learns that she's been requested to write Jake's bio. She will have to go on tour with The Mighty Storm in Europe and the US. She takes this opportunity and from this love blossoms, jealousy rears it's head, heartbreak is a given and everything that entails with the lifestyle...drugs, sex and rock-n-roll. And the visuals I got from Jake and his "snake"...Good God Almighty! I love my imagination.<br /><br />I will say this. There is a part in the book that deals with Jake's addiction to drugs that was an emotional rollercoaster. Very heartbreaking.<br /><br />Favorite moments/lines:<br /><br />The first concert after Jonny's death and the tribute they give him. *tear*<br /><br />"And that's why I prefer to dance in the bedroom."<br /><br />"It's always been you, Tru. Always."<br /><br />"You look beautiful," he says.<br />"And you look like an idiot, get up, I say, suppressing the huge smile I feel.<br /><br />"You. Then, and now. How beautiful you were back then, and how even more beautiful you are now. How I wish I'd seen you through all those years, and how I'm counting myself as one lucky bastard that I got a second chance to have you in my life...and that you're crazy enough to be mine."<br /><br /><br />At the end of the story there's a part called Meet Jake...Chapter One-The Hotel, where we get his POV. Now with this I would love to get the rest of his POV. Aaaaand hopefully more on Tru and Jake. </span>
  <a data-text-id="9693307996785759218" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer12631773878971815764"><i>Re-read 4th - 5th August 2013</i><br/>***************************<br/><b>“He is the ultimate bad boy of rock.”</b><br/><br/>I decided to spend a little time with an old book boyfriend and indulged myself in a delicious re-read. <i>I want to be ready for Jake and the release of the hotly anticipated </i>~ <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16053316.Wethering_the_Storm__The_Storm___2_' title='Wethering the Storm (The Storm, #2) by Samantha Towle' rel='nofollow noopener'>Wethering The Storm</a><br/><br/>♥<img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406678i/793746._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Am I setting the scene?</i> <br/><br/>A love triangle…....<br/><br/>Stable long term, loving boyfriend <br/><blockquote>

</blockquote>An old friend......bad boy rocker.......alpha in the extreme….....A Rock Star?????? <br/><br/>♥ ♥ ♥<br/><br/>Both the hero and the heroin</span>
  <span id="freeText12631773878971815764" style="display:none"><i>Re-read 4th - 5th August 2013</i><br>***************************<br><b>“He is the ultimate bad boy of rock.”</b><br><br>I decided to spend a little time with an old book boyfriend and indulged myself in a delicious re-read. <i>I want to be ready for Jake and the release of the hotly anticipated </i>~ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16053316.Wethering_the_Storm__The_Storm___2_" title="Wethering the Storm (The Storm, #2) by Samantha Towle" rel="nofollow noopener">Wethering The Storm</a><br><br>♥<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380406678i/793746._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Am I setting the scene?</i> <br><br>A love triangle…....<br><br>Stable long term, loving boyfriend <br><blockquote>
  <b>verses......</b>
</blockquote>An old friend......bad boy rocker.......alpha in the extreme….....A Rock Star?????? <br><br>♥ ♥ ♥<br><br>Both the hero and the heroine are wonderful characters and as the reader you WANT so much for them....read it (if you haven't already) and you will see! Jake is gorgeous and Tru, well, she'd make a great best friend. ♥ The Mighty Storm takes you on a delicious journey and makes you feel so much...it has it all, <i>
  <b>LOVE, PAIN, ANGST, SEX, CONFLICT, TEARS, HEARTBREAK </b>
</i>.....it makes my heart warm and sad and happy.......simply a stunning read and one that I'm sure I'll devour again and again. <br><br>♥ If you love a rock star than this, in my opinion is one of the greats!!!! <b>
  <i>YOU WILL LOVE JAKE!!!!</i>

<div id="review_399766971" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/399766971" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/399766971?book_show_action=true">Aug 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=omg-romantic">omg-romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=feeeeels">feeeeels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=rockers">rockers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-book-1">series-book-1</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=pb-i-own-signed">pb-i-own-signed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series-faves-book-1">series-faves-book-1</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer399766971" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5092980326495821821">So awesome, ridiculously swoony and heaps of emotion. <br/><b>I FREAKING LOVED THIS BOOK!</b><br/><br/>Jake Wethers is a heavily tattooed, uber-hot, Alpha rock God, and I absolutely adored him! Tru is the girl who grew up next to him – childhood best friends, they were each other’s first loves, although Jake’s family moved away before anything could happen between them. When they are reunited 12 years later, the emotional connection is still there, along with an intense chemistry that doesn’t let up the entire book.<br/><br/>T</span>
  <span id="freeText5092980326495821821" style="display:none">So awesome, ridiculously swoony and heaps of emotion. <br /><b>I FREAKING LOVED THIS BOOK!</b><br /><br />Jake Wethers is a heavily tattooed, uber-hot, Alpha rock God, and I absolutely adored him! Tru is the girl who grew up next to him – childhood best friends, they were each other’s first loves, although Jake’s family moved away before anything could happen between them. When they are reunited 12 years later, the emotional connection is still there, along with an intense chemistry that doesn’t let up the entire book.<br /><br />Told from Tru’s POV, the story moves at a great pace, and things develop really quickly. Yes, there are the inevitable similarities to Thoughtless, but this book is amazing all on its own. What I loved about this relationship is that Jake and Tru actually deal with what’s going on between them. The issue of ‘the other guy’ is dealt with fairly quickly and through it all they are honest with each other. Yes, there are moments of stupid but it doesn’t last too long. <br /><br />The thing that stands out for me in this story is the way I felt while reading it. The emotional scenes in this book are amazing! I was buddy reading, and at a particularly intense moment around halfway through, the number of emails flying back and forth with the word “FUUUUUUCK” in them was downright ridiculous! My heart was pounding – I was shocked, I wanted to cheer, I wanted to swoon. At other times my heart broke - for Will, for Tru, and for Jake - and I’d find myself in floods of tears, only to be grinning like an idiot and hugging my kindle a few pages later. It was an intense rollercoaster, and I loved every minute of it!<br /><br />Although there are some serious issues dealt with in the story (fidelity, death, addiction, and dealing with the celebrity lifestyle), it’s not all heavy. It’s primarily a romance, and there are lots of gorgeously sweet moments (Jake is such a romantic!), as well as heaps of swoon. There were also lots of funny scenes – particularly with Jake’s bandmates. Their banter was crude but hilarious, and I loved the close relationship that they obviously shared. <br /><br />Read this book if you want an incredibly emotional, beautifully romantic (and somewhat steamy) story. The only negative thing I have to say is that I thought the ending was too abrupt, I wanted more - although rumour has it there will be a sequel. Squeeee!! Must.have.more!!!<br /><br /><br />Oh, and a quick shout out to the little extra at the end of the book - the reunion scene from Jake's POV. It was HILARIOUS getting inside of his head, and really gave us a good idea of what he was feeling, and how quickly and how deeply he felt it. Great little addition to the story!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5092980326495821821" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_415159046" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/415159046" />
    <a title="Jen " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5962787-jen"><img alt="Jen " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1563496869p2/5962787.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/415159046?book_show_action=true">Sep 15, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen " href="/user/show/5962787-jen">Jen </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer415159046" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10823553098570101893">I liked but not loved this book. As a way to pass the time on a still too hot to play tennis like I wanted to Sunday, it wasn’t half bad. I guess my issues with this one stem mostly from the fact that it was a “tell not show” kind of read and I was hoping for something else based on the reviews of this book. He looked at her intensely. She wanted him with an intensity like she’d never felt. She looked into his eyes and saw (you guessed it) intense lust. I get it…their feelings are all kinds of i</span>
  <span id="freeText10823553098570101893" style="display:none">I liked but not loved this book. As a way to pass the time on a still too hot to play tennis like I wanted to Sunday, it wasn’t half bad. I guess my issues with this one stem mostly from the fact that it was a “tell not show” kind of read and I was hoping for something else based on the reviews of this book. He looked at her intensely. She wanted him with an intensity like she’d never felt. She looked into his eyes and saw (you guessed it) intense lust. I get it…their feelings are all kinds of intense and various other adjectives of the sort, but the problem for me is that there’s only one real love scene and I wouldn’t describe it as strong as it needed to be for the type of feelings these two were supposedly carrying around during their 12 year separation. Pretty standard stuff, actually, for a super hot rock star and the only lady he’s ever loved. Everything else was alluded to. Don’t get me wrong, I’m not saying I need every book to be a constant sex fest. Far from it. Sometimes Tru’s love for Will came across as stronger than the love she felt for Jake. Since I wasn’t feeling WHY these two were soul mates or why Jake was as possessive from the get go as he was, I guess I just needed a little something extra to show me. Other than a nighttime trip to one of their favorite childhood hangouts and a super classy Paris date there wasn’t much else. Their issues resolve themselves way too easily by the end and I felt this entire book just could’ve been more. </span>
  <a data-text-id="10823553098570101893" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('MeGonQ/kiWZXJY0nDpsrWtqhLJ3kCJDgojUNNbSdTlv7/Y+/8oqOcN7LGzGC3A5jRIRi9hfmYXYwnE/eJ0mwVA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('mTmiBFQTIhCGOOmWMo5RuteAaQ58Fy66FBzSvrQCcxlTJYUmqX0lBg/Wf4C+yXSDSaUnZY/53yyGtZBVJ9aNFg==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer11577990744923318941">Samantha Towle is a New York Times, USA Today, and Wall Street Journal bestselling author. <br/><br/>A native of Hull, she lives in East Yorkshire with her husband, their son and daughter, and three large furbabies.<br/><br/>She is the author of contemporary romances, The Storm Series, The Revved Series, The Wardrobe Series, The Gods Series, and standalones, Trouble, When I Was Yours, The Ending I Want, Unsuitable, U</span>
  <span id="freeText11577990744923318941" style="display:none">Samantha Towle is a New York Times, USA Today, and Wall Street Journal bestselling author. <br /><br />A native of Hull, she lives in East Yorkshire with her husband, their son and daughter, and three large furbabies.<br /><br />She is the author of contemporary romances, The Storm Series, The Revved Series, The Wardrobe Series, The Gods Series, and standalones, Trouble, When I Was Yours, The Ending I Want, Unsuitable, Under Her, River Wild and Sacking the Quarterback which was written with James Patterson. She has also written paranormal romances, The Bringer and The Alexandra Jones Series.
